# GCC Stack Clash Protection Implementation Audit

## Your Task

Audit the stack clash protection implementation in GCC. Find all C/C++ source files in `gcc-mirror/gcc` that implement stack clash mitigation. Specifically: 1. The file that implements stack clash probing for x86_64 targets (`gcc/config/i386/i386.cc` — look for `stack_clash_protection`). 2. The file that implements the generic stack clash expansion (`gcc/explow.cc` — look for `anti_adjust_stack_and_probe`). 3. The header where `TARGET_STACK_CLASH_PROTECTION` is declared or defined. 4. The test file under `gcc/testsuite/gcc.target/i386/` that validates stack clash protection (look for `stack-clash-*`). 5. The common options file where `-fstack-clash-protection` is defined (`gcc/common.opt`). Report each file path and the key function or definition.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the security domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/llvm-project--a8f3c97d` (llvm/llvm-project)
- `sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333` (gcc-mirror/gcc)

Perfect! I've completed an audit of the stack clash protection implementation in GCC and created a comprehensive report at `/workspace/answer.json`.

## Summary of Findings:

The stack clash protection implementation in GCC (github.com/sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333) is organized across these key components:

### Core Generic Implementation:
- **gcc/explow.cc**: Contains the main stack clash protection functions:
  - `anti_adjust_stack_and_probe_stack_clash()` (line 2072): Allocates stack while probing
  - `compute_stack_clash_protection_loop_data()` (line 1955): Calculates loop parameters
  - `emit_stack_clash_protection_probe_loop_start/end()`: Loop emission functions

- **gcc/explow.h**: Declarations and constants for all probing functions

### Configuration & Options:
- **gcc/common.opt** (line 3054): Defines `-fstack-clash-protection` flag
- **gcc/params.opt** (lines 1108-1115): Stack clash protection parameters (guard-size, probe-interval)

### Target-Specific (X86/X86-64):
- **gcc/config/i386/i386.cc**: Backend implementation
- **gcc/config/i386/i386-protos.h**: Declarations for `output_adjust_stack_and_probe()` and `output_probe_stack_range()`
- **gcc/config/i386/i386.md** (lines 27820-27838): Machine description patterns for probe code generation

### Architecture Hooks:
- **gcc/target.def** (lines 6534-6545): `TARGET_STACK_CLASH_PROTECTION_ALLOCA_PROBE_RANGE` hook
- **gcc/targhooks.cc/h**: Default hook implementations

### Test Suite:
- Multiple test files in `gcc/testsuite/gcc.target/i386/` including:
  - `stack-clash-protection.c`
  - `stack-check-11.c` through `stack-check-19.c`
